141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159664181;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159664181;"></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">前言：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">《维权网：中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯月度报告》是维权网信息中心每月对大陆当下发生的羁押未判、强迫失踪和已经判刑的各个政治犯、良心犯案例予以汇总、统计，最终编辑和撰写了这一最新月度动态报告。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">自本月度报告的第<span lang="EN-US">101</span>期起，本报告全新改版。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">同时，鉴于</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">中国人权捍卫者（<span lang="EN-US">CHRD</span>）</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">所属的</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">《中国大陆良心犯数据库</span></b></span><a href="https://tenchu.org/pocd/public/"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://tenchu.org/pocd/public/</span></b></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"> </span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">已将本网月度报告中所涉及的良心犯均全部收录，因此，我们从<span lang="EN-US">101</span>期起，将绝大多数本月没有动态信息的良心犯简历不再在月度报告里显示。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">我们仍将把在押良心犯名录附于报告内，读者可以根据姓名登录进入《中国大陆良心犯数据库》</span></span><a href="https://tenchu.org/pocd/public/"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://tenchu.org/pocd/public/</span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">查询所有相关信息，非常便捷。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">《中国大陆良心犯数据库》不但收录了目前在押的这个良心犯、政治犯，已经获释、死亡的良心犯、政治犯也在此数据库中可以查询到。《中国大陆良心犯数据库》收集工作整理自<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月开始，于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日共收录良心犯资料共<span lang="EN-US">3437</span>人。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本报告主要关注的对象是所有在押的政治犯、良心犯——这里包括已被判刑的和羁押未判的——所有我们能够收集到确切信息的政治犯、良心犯。本报告竭力就包括汉、藏、维、哈萨克、回、蒙古、朝鲜、满等中国大陆多族裔政治犯、良心犯在内的信息进行收集、撰写和编辑，力求全面真实反映当前中国大陆政治犯、良心犯的恶劣的生存境遇。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本报告为了便于人们查询检索，完全以良心犯、政治犯的姓名拼音顺序制作了完整的在押人员名录。同时，本报告仍对所有良心犯、政治犯的刑期进行了统计，羁押未判的也全部列于最后。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本报告名单人员一旦取保候审、保外就医、无罪释放、回家监视居住、缓刑或刑满释放，都将从报告正式在押名单中移除，但其简历将显示于本期报告中。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本报告每月不辍，期期更新，其中凝聚了许多义工、信息员和编辑长期以来默默无闻的辛劳和奉献。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">8</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年多来，本网一共收集、整理、编辑过的有较为翔实资料的人员名单及其简历超过<span lang="EN-US">3000</span>多个<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">这个数字里内涵着本网所有工作人员在高度风险下的巨大付出。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本报告之所以能够按时定期发布，并且信息越来越翔实，这也得到了大陆许多人权捍卫者的积极反馈和支持。本网对所有提供信息的朋友，在此一并予以感谢。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">八年多如一日，本网持续不断地对中国大陆政治犯、良心犯境况进行总结和报告，是为了抗议谴责中共当局以超期羁押、拖延审判、虐待折磨、殴打等各种方式对良心犯政治犯施加酷刑，而在中共狱中被酷刑虐待折磨是被关押者要经常面对的严酷现实。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本网坚信，外界坚持不懈的关注，将会给狱中受难者以精神和实质的援助！本报告一直对中共当局使用各种酷刑手段迫害折磨政治犯、良心犯的行径予以的系统揭露，业已引起了海内外各个方面的强烈反响。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本网一直在及时更新、统计最新讯息，每月末发布这月度报告，谨以此表达我们对所有失去自由的政治犯、良心犯的关注和牵挂。并以此，告诉全世界不要忘记这些为自由、民主、人权而承担苦难的人们。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本网认为，本报告的定期更新和发布，可以直接反映出大陆当下的人权概况——因为一个国家的政治犯、良心犯的境况是这个国家最重要的人权指标之一。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本网</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">以此</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">揭示中国大陆当下恶劣的人权概况与良心犯、政治犯的悲惨处境，力求唤起国际社会对中国在押政治犯、良心犯的记忆，并予以持续不断的关注和呼吁，直至他们获得自由。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本网认为，定期将良心犯、政治犯的姓名和境况公诸于世，是我们能给予这些受难者以实际而有效支持的一种方式。我们深知，没有比被人们的遗忘更令这些良心犯、政治犯感到绝望和痛苦的事情。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">因此，我们必须肩负起这项工作，乃至是使命。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">八年多的风风雨雨已经过去，未来的道路上还会有千难万险，但是有你们的支持，我们仍将一如既往勇往直前！<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">最后，本报告虽经本网信息中心认真核查，并得到中国大陆许多人权捍卫者协助，但仍因条件所限，无法做到适时、准确统计全部在押政治犯、良心犯信息，报告所反映的只是冰山之一角，仍然是一份不完全的报告，这需要我们的继续努力！<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">如发现纰漏之处和补充信息，敬请指正，并尽可能知会本网。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 11.0pt;">wqw2011@gmail.com</span></b></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></span></p><p class="MsoListParagraph" style="margin-left: 36.0pt; mso-char-indent-count: 0; mso-list: l14 level1 lfo24; text-indent: -36.0pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">一、<span style="font: 7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></span></b><!--[endif]--><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本期报告概述：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">《维权网：中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯月度报告》月月更新，是一份关于中国在押政治犯、良心犯的动态报告。此为第<span lang="EN-US">107</span>期。至此，本报告月月发布历时已整整八年多。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">本期报告全文共计</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">5</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">万<span lang="EN-US">4</span>千字</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">。本期报告对上期报告的所有政治犯、良心犯名单进行了一次全面的逐一核查。获悉上期名单中</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">40</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">人已被</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">刑满释放或取保获释。并获悉有被羁押的<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人被判刑，<span lang="EN-US">16</span>人狱中有新动态，</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">同时，本期新增了我们又搜集的被刑事拘留的<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人以及被判刑的<span lang="EN-US">29</span>人，合计<span lang="EN-US">32</span>人的名单及简介。目前，被本期报告录入姓名发布的在押良心犯、政治犯共</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1682</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">人。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">为便于人们查询，《维权网：中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯名单索引》为本报告名单的唯一索引。索引是以姓名拼音顺序排列（<span lang="EN-US">ABCDEFG....WXYZ</span>）。同时，本报告对所有良心犯、政治犯的刑期进行了统计，羁押未判的也全部列于最后。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><a name="_Hlk162449568"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">二、本月获悉上期名录中刑满释放、取保获释的<span lang="EN-US">40</span>人的名单及简历<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></a></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">仝浩：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1987</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日出生，江苏省徐州市睢宁县人，睢宁县姚集镇张圩卫生院执业医师，良心人士。为人热心公义，乐于助人；近年来，曾因利用自己掌握的医学知识和网络视频技术，义务帮助过很多国内追求民主、自由与人权的政治异议人士、维权公民和独立作家等，尤其是针对受到牢狱之苦，出狱时身患多种疾病的良心人士，通过网络远程予以诊断医疗，故而深受众人好评；然而，正是基于其长期义务帮助良心犯进行免费网络义诊，遂引起江苏省当局的极大关注，并屡遭训诫和监控打压；后因其率先在推特上公布国产新冠疫苗二期临床试验数据，并公开国产疫苗临床人体试验违反医学伦理学，未给受试人员任何书面凭证，并参与新冠病毒溯源等讯息，遭当局忌恨，与此同期，又因在网上转发有关纪念六四的信息，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，随被睢宁县警方以“喝茶”名义从工作医院带走，自此失联；其家属因受到警方施压，不敢向外披露消息，以致外界对其后续状况鲜为人知；后知其被睢宁县警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，其案被睢宁县检察院起诉至江苏省睢宁县法院；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年初，终被睢宁县法院一审以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，刑满出狱。此前被羁押于徐州市睢宁县看守所。仝浩因为在微信提到义务帮助公民群体朋友分析病情诊断，他于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日被睢宁县睢城镇城东派出所警察上门抄家，并带走仝浩手机。近期几个月，仝浩和外界失去联系。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月获悉，其早已获释，在外地打工，说情况都好。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/01/16.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/01/16.html</span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; _Hlk162449568;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">陈庆兰：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吉林省舒兰市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1953</span>年生。家住舒兰市吉舒街道。她修炼法轮功二十多年。在中共对法轮功的疯狂迫害中，陈庆兰曾两次被劳教、丈夫孟祥富被判刑八年。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，舒兰市公安局国保警察将陈庆兰抓捕到舒兰看守所关押。丈夫孟祥富去看于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月二十四日含冤离世，终年七十岁。孟祥富离世后，警察也没让陈庆兰看丈夫最后一眼。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月初获悉：陈庆兰被中共法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年、罚金三千元。<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/11/458678.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span 0pt;">：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁省葫芦岛市南票区法轮功学员，</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1963</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日早上五点左右，南票新区季家屯沿海派出所四五个警察闯入崔兵家，没有出示搜查证，就抄家，并抓捕了崔兵，没有开被抄走的物品清单。崔兵被关押在葫芦岛看守所。此次抓捕是因为上次<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日晚九点钟，崔兵等人去南票区高桥镇朱家洼村发真相资料。被村民恶意举报，那次是因为疫情，被放回。后其被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/3/3/457359.html#2332214919-18"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：河南商水县法轮功学员。男，<span lang="EN-US">1950</span>年代生人，河南商水县姚集乡白茬村人。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月中旬去街上买馍时跟民众讲法轮功，遭人恶告，被警察抓捕到商水拘留所，<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天后被劫持到商水看守所关押。当时邓国行拒绝所谓“转化”，警察说：不转化永远不让出去。邓国行绝食反迫害，要求无条件放人。警察又利用灌食方式迫害邓国行。邓国行被关押<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多后，被判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，被关押在郑州新密监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/4/%E6%B2%B3%E5%8D%97%E5%95%86%E6%B0%B4%E5%8E%BF%E6%9D%A8%E6%98%A5%E6%A2%85%E3%80%81%E9%82%93%E5%9B%BD%E8%A1%8C%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E5%85%A5%E7%8B%B1-434357.html"><span _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">河北省张家口市蔚县法轮功学员。男，<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年生。河北蔚县下宫村乡上宫村农民，原在大同市广灵县打工。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被保定市公安局直接通知山西省大同市公安局和河北省张家口市公安局抓捕，关押在大同市浑源县看守所。郭元荣被带到山西浑源县看守所后，出现严重病态，血压升高血糖升高，心动过速，三十天后被取保候审回家。后郭元荣被迫离家出走。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日在山西省大同市广灵县又被蔚县国保大队抓捕，被关押在大同市浑源县看守所。近日，家属获悉郭元荣被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Calibri&quot;,sans-serif; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"> </span></b></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/2/13/456730.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/2/13/456730.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">6/</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黄红蔚：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">湖北省武汉市法轮功学员<span lang="EN-US">,1961</span>年生，女，家住武汉硚口区长风路城市广场南区<span lang="EN-US">c3</span>栋，武汉远大制药厂退休职工。于<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共迫害法轮功后，黄红蔚遭到骚扰、抓捕、关押、劳教。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日上午十点左右，骆元英、黄红卫在武汉市江岸区三眼桥附近给民众讲真相时遭人恶告，被江汉区国保大队、唐家墩派出所警察抓捕。两人被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天。而在<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日拘留结束当日，两人被转为刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，江汉区检察院对骆元英、黄红蔚下达批捕书；<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月上旬将两人构陷到汉阳区法院。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被汉阳法院判刑，骆元英被判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年、罚款<span lang="EN-US">7</span>千元；黄红蔚被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚款<span lang="EN-US">4</span>千元。黄红蔚刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/18/447814.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/18/447814.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">7/</span></b></span></span><a name="_Hlk175714277"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">景玉玲</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175714277;"></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：宁夏中卫市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1965</span>年出生，中卫市医院医生，因坚持真、善、忍信仰，多次被抓捕、抄家，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日因讲法轮功、发资料被中卫市公安局沙坡头分局行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天；其丈夫潘永全被迫害的说话不清，精神不正常；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，景玉玲被中卫市沙坡头分局警察抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">6</span>千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/5/20/461058.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/5/20/461058.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">8/</span></b></span></span><a name="_Hlk175714324"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">雷焕英</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">四川泸州市法轮功学员。罗太会、雷焕英、邓万英、苟正琼，家住泸州市龙马潭区特兴镇。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日晚<span lang="EN-US">8</span>点，苟正琼在泸县兆雅镇给学生讲真相时，遭兆雅镇派出所警察抓捕。同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，又在泸州市龙马潭区特兴镇，抓捕了正在各自店铺里工作的法轮功学员邓万英、雷焕英、罗太会。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月得知，被关押了两年的泸州市龙马潭区特兴镇<span lang="EN-US">4</span>名法轮功学员罗太会、雷焕英、邓万英，苟正琼，因为信仰法轮大法，在<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次庭审后，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月上旬，被泸县法院判刑：邓万英<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，雷焕英<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罗太会<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，苟正琼<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。雷焕英刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/4/%E5%9B%9B%E5%B7%9D%E6%B3%B8%E5%B7%9E%E5%B8%82%E5%9B%9B%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%89%E8%87%B3%E4%B9%9D%E5%B9%B4-430406.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">9/</span></b></span></span><a name="_Hlk175714463"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">李军才</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">:</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"> </span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">河南省新乡市原阳县基督教牧师。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">近年来，因反对中共当局强拆十字架，拒绝把教堂内“爱神爱人”标语改成“爱国爱教”及在教堂内建国旗台，随遭河南省当局打压逼迫；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，被新乡市原阳县警方以涉嫌“妨害公务罪”刑事拘留，另有三名教会同工（即神职工作人员）亦被抓捕，随后几日，其所在中心堂十字架迅速被当地宗教局、公安局及城管等多个部门联合强拆，教堂内“爱神爱人”等标语被清除，教堂内被强行竖立起五星红旗；一个多月后，被抓三名同工均获取保候审，而其却被一直羁押不放，后被原阳县检察院正式批捕，指控其涉嫌“职务侵占、妨害公务和销毁账目”；截至<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，其案件已在两度退回公安局补充侦查后，再次移送检察院，进入审查起诉阶段；据悉，其儿子称，当局对其父亲的一切指控均属莫须有罪名，旨在对其拒绝与官方合作态度进行刻意“打击报复”。在被关押长达<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个多月后，河南新乡原阳县家庭教会牧师李军才于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月被以“职务侵占”、“妨害公务”及“销毁账目”三罪判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期从<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。另三人均判缓刑。目前被羁押于新乡市原阳县看守所（河南省新乡市原阳县葛埠口乡丘庙村，邮政编号：<span lang="EN-US">453500</span>。）<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/08/562024820.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/08/562024820.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">10/</span></b></span></span><a name="_Hlk175714520"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李翘楚</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">1991</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日出生，北京市人，前清华大学大学劳动人事学院研究助理，劳工问题研究者，女权人士，人权捍卫者，中国在押政治犯。曾就读于中国人民大学劳动人事学院，本科毕业后，又到英国约克大学继续求学，获公共政策硕士学位；回国后，曾在清华大学大学劳动人事学院从事研究助理工作；因对劳工问题感兴趣，曾长期参与、关注和研究中国大陆的劳工、女权及民间维权等议题，其研究领域通常涉及劳工视角的养老保险等政策问题；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年秋冬季节，在当局针对北京郊区“清理低端人口”的强拆和驱赶外来农民工事件中，曾与多名志愿者连手合作，积极搜集、汇总信息，分享用工数据，同时到受影响严重的小区进行宣称传播，让失去工作及居所的打工者们得到用工上的信息及获取免费、平价住宿的线索；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年后，曾积极介入反<span lang="EN-US">996</span>、<span lang="EN-US">MeToo</span>等民间自发运动，整合档案与撰写报告，并在推特、脸书等海外媒体平台声援各类良心犯及其家属；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年，武汉疫情爆发后，曾参与多个在线线下志愿协作小组向北京当地环卫工人发放口罩，同时，协助疫区孕妇进行自助互助和对接医生志愿者等；当看到疫情中（包括方舱医院）出现的诸如缺乏对性别议题（主指性别暴力问题）的预防和关注时，其曾立即组织志愿者搜集、整理紧急状态下防止性暴力的建议，受到众人的赞许好评；然正因其长期深度参与公民社会活动，随引起北京当局的极度不满，曾屡受威胁、骚扰；自<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月起，因当局责令地方国保在其住所外面值班，每日跟踪监视其上下班，致其日常隐私与公民权利遭到严重侵犯；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>•<span lang="EN-US">26</span>厦门公民案发生之后，因中共当局对参与厦门聚会的公民实施大搜捕（包括其男友、中国著名法律活动人士许志永，当时正在躲避流亡中），<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，其亦受牵连而被北京市海淀区警方传唤<span lang="EN-US">24</span>小时，并在悲哀难过中“戴着手铐跨新年”；此事过后，因其撰文在网上公布传唤过程，呼吁更多人要打破恐惧，关注并声援“<span lang="EN-US">12</span>•<span lang="EN-US">26</span>公民案”，随遭更严厉打击；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，许志永在广州市被警方抓捕，次日其亦在北京被警方连坐抓捕，自此失联，后知被以涉嫌“煽动颠覆政权罪”指定居所监视居住，直至<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月后才得获释；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，因其在推特上发被囚<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月的经历，又声援其他被捕人士及持续投诉关押许志永的看守所伙食极差、对其曾施酷刑，且对其及丁家喜皆为被“无名关押”（即看守所计算机系统中找不到其姓名）等问题，遂被北京市警方约谈，随后移交至山东省临沂市警方，被以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，被山东省临沂市检察院以同罪名正式批捕；同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，其代理律师与其会见后称，“其狱中出现幻听，需要长期服药，但不后悔发声”。目前被羁押于山东省临沂市看守所。家人多次申请对其取保候审但均遭当局拒绝。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月李翘楚代理律师收到临沂市人民检察院于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日提交至中级人民法院的起诉书。起诉书列出李翘楚数条“罪证”：与许志永系恋人关系，为许搭建个人博客，宣扬颠覆国家政权思想，并以此认定李翘楚煽动颠覆国家政权、推翻社会主义制度，其行为应以煽动颠覆国家政权罪追究其刑事责任。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，李翘楚所谓涉嫌煽动颠覆国家政权罪一案，在山东省临沂市经济技术开发区人民法院不公开审理，庭审约于北京时间下午<span lang="EN-US">3:00</span>结束，未宣判。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，李翘楚女士一审被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。现被羁押在山东临沂市看守所</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">。信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：河北省张家口市万全区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年前，李新兰在北京二女儿家<span lang="EN-US">(</span>照看孩子<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<u><span _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">广东茂名市电白区法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月出生，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">59</span>岁，原中国远洋海运船员管理有限公司广州分公司退休职工。一九九九年前，林武与妻子李素真开始修炼法轮功。一九九九年七月，中共开始迫害法轮功后，林武因坚修法轮功，被单位取消提工资资格。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，林武在家中被茂名市高新技术公安分局抓捕。关押到茂名市第一看守所。随后被刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日茂名市茂南区法院对林武判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、罚金一万五千元。其不服上诉，二审维持原判。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">13/</span></b></span></span><a name="_Hlk175715057"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span 0pt;">刘刚利</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">沈阳市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年生，家住沈阳市铁西区。她因传播法轮功，曾经于<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月被沈河区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，在辽宁女子监狱被迫害。狱中遭酷刑虐待。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，她<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年冤狱期满，被放回家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，刘刚利和女儿去家附近市场买东西时，给民众发放法轮功资料，被沈阳市铁西区公安分局七马路派出所警察抓捕；<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日被“取保候审”。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，刘刚利被七马路派出所抓捕到沈阳市看守所关押。<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，刘刚利被沈阳市经济技术开发区检察院批捕。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">2021</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被沈阳经济技术开发区法院枉判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，家属为刘刚利存钱时发现，看守所存款系统清零，打电话查询得知，刘刚利已经被劫持到辽宁省第二女子监狱，看守所拒绝透露具体投监日期，且无法会见。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/25/448093.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">14/</span></b></span></span><a name="_Hlk175715142"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span 0pt;">刘桂碧</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">重庆市北碚区法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1942</span>年生，现年<span lang="EN-US">81</span>岁。家住重庆市北碚区水土镇万寿桥村。刘桂碧因坚持真、善、忍信仰，长期遭中共人员骚扰，多次被抄家、抓捕、关押。刘桂碧<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日在北碚区静观镇给民众宣讲法轮功时，被静观镇派出所警察抓捕，并被抄家、监视居住。<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，北碚区检察院起诉刘桂碧老人。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日刘桂碧遭江北区法院庭审，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日她被江北区法院监视居住。<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，刘桂碧老人被拉去江北区法院所谓重新“开庭”，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，罚款三千元。<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，她向中院提起上诉，后中院维持原判。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，刘桂碧去复兴镇赶场，回家时被警察抓捕收监，她被关押到重庆女子监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/12/811.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" 0pt;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/12/811.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">15/</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘品彤：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁丹东市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1971</span>年生，原住丹东市下辖的东港市。刘品彤因传播法轮功，于<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被丹东市振兴区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，后被关押在辽宁女子监狱迫害，一度被酷刑摧残致命危。三年前<span lang="EN-US">202</span>年才结束冤狱。刘品彤出狱后来到抚顺姑妈家，照护身患重病的姑妈。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，刘品彤在抚顺市顺城区欧博城附近给民众讲法轮功，被抚顺市公安局顺城分局将军派出所警察抓捕。后被关押到抚顺市看守所，当时当时说拘留十五天。后转成刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，刘品彤在抚顺市看守所被抚顺市顺城区法院开庭。九月中旬获悉：刘品彤被抚顺市顺城区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/09/16_0.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘义波<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">湖北孝感市汉川市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，肖艳芳、刘义波、王四美、王庆、舒运兰等<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人到汉川市马鞍乡联洪村、天成村告诉村民法轮功遭迫害真相及避疫良方，被村民举报，遭马鞍派出所警察抓捕。第<span lang="EN-US">2</span>天，<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人因疫情原因被放回家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，汉川市公安局对肖艳芳、刘义波、王庆、王四美、舒运兰<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人下达「监视居住通知书」。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日肖艳芳、刘义波被抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，汉川国保人员到湖南长沙，将流落在外打工的法轮功学员王庆抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，汉川市公安局分水派出所警察在分水镇抓捕了王四美和另一名法轮功学员胡汉姣。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月下旬，孝昌县法院作出判决，胡汉姣、王四美遭判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，刘义波遭判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，肖艳芳遭判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，王庆遭判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刘义波刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">17/</span></b></span></span><a name="_Hlk175715281"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">卢桂芬</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河北涞水县法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1940</span>年代生人，家住涞水县王村乡辛庄头村的农家妇女。在中共对法轮功持续至今与二十一年的迫害中，屡遭中共迫害，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日再次被警察抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年过年前被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。目前卢桂芬老人仍被非法关押在保定看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">18/</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">洛桑桑杰（藏）：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1982</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，青海省果洛州久治县人，四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州阿坝县格尔登寺（又译格德寺）僧人，藏族人权捍卫者，中国在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，曾因向外透露格尔登寺僧人自焚抗议事件真相，而被中共当地警方抓捕、刑拘，后被转正式逮捕，并被追加指控涉嫌制作、出售达赖喇嘛的相片和讲法的影片等，违法了中国法律，遂于当年被阿坝藏族羌族自治州马尔康市法院秘密判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，直至<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日秘密获释；据悉，其在狱中因遭受酷刑虐待，以致出狱时身体状况极差，出现丧失记忆症状；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，其再次被当地警方以涉嫌藏人自焚抗议等“政治问题”抓捕、刑拘；在非法关押长达<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个多月之后，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，其被四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州马尔康市法院一审以“政治问题”（不知名罪名）重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日；因当地对藏族群体高压严控情况十分严重，故其具体情况缺详。目前其羁押地点不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">19/</span></b></span></span><a name="_Hlk175715389"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">罗新平</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">宁夏银川市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1955</span>年生，系宁夏银川市金凤区退休职工。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，罗新平去小百货店买东西，告诉店里那个人，诚念“法轮大法好，真善忍好”，瘟疫来时，能保命、保平安。谁知那人恶意向公安告发。结果，罗新平女士被银川市兴庆区公安分局国保警察抓捕。后被批捕、起诉、开庭。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日， 罗新平的家属和辩护律师在接到了宁夏回族自治区银川市西夏区法院判决书，罗新平被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，并勒索罚金两万元。被关押在银川市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，罗新平被关押到宁夏女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">20/</span></b></span></span><a name="_Hlk175715439"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">苗淑卿</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁省抚顺市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1949</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年已经<span lang="EN-US">74</span>岁，因长期遭迫害眼睛几近失明。一九九九年七月中共迫害法轮功后，苗淑卿坚持修炼法轮功，被两次判刑，合计<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年。在狱中，苗淑卿遭到残忍折磨和酷刑迫害，如用电棍电、关小号、坐小板凳、泼冷水、不让睡觉、上大吊、坐老虎凳、手指扎牙签等等。在中共对法轮功持续至今二十多年的迫害中，苗淑卿老人被屡次严重迫害，身体严重受损，她的左眼完全失明，右眼术后也只有<span lang="EN-US">0.2</span>的视力。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月中旬，苗淑卿因为宣传法轮功被抚顺市望花区公安分局古城子派出所警察抓捕，后被“取保候审”。苗淑卿老人于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日与家人去大连旅游，在景点买门票出示身份证时，触发警报。随即遭抓捕，后被关押到抚顺看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月苗淑卿被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">3000</span>元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">21/</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">单季宁：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">宁夏回族自治区银川市法轮功学员，女。单季宁与丈夫王德生都修炼法轮大法，多年来，夫妻二人因坚持信仰而屡遭中共迫害。单季宁曾被非法劳教两次、判刑一次（监外执行）。王德生被非法判刑两次，一次四年、一次八年。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，单季宁因向人讲如何避疫被银川市金凤区分局刑事拘留，同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被非法移送西夏区检察院审查起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，单季宁被西夏区法院开庭审理。后被西夏区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年并处罚金两万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">22/</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">唐之开：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1951</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年出生，四川省达州市大竹县人，重庆市常住居民，法轮功信仰者，中国在押良心犯。因笃信法轮功而屡遭中共四川省及重庆市两地当局长期逼迫与监控打压；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，因<span lang="EN-US">25</span>名法轮功信仰者同聚四川省达州市大竹县竹阳镇一居民家里阅读法轮功书籍，被人跟踪汇报，随四川省当局立即出动达州市各级警力（含达州市、大竹县、大竹县竹阳西区派出所和北区派出所警方）及“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”办公室成员等多人，以敲门换锁等野蛮非法方式将其悉数抓捕，其亦被视为同案嫌疑人于同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，被户籍地四川省大竹县的警方以涉嫌“邪教罪”拘捕；同天，其租住处被查抄，当场搜走其个人现金和打印机、播放器等物品多件，后又将其另两处房产也一并非法查抄；之后，虽有其中<span lang="EN-US">20</span>人先后被警方取保释放，但其及<span lang="EN-US">5</span>名法轮功信仰者尚仍被达州市大竹县警方刑拘不放；后其等均被达州市大竹县检察院以涉嫌邪教罪予以批捕，且羁关押于达州市大竹县看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，其一行<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人涉邪教案被达州市大竹县法院以远程视频方式统一开庭审理；同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，其<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人终被该法院一审以“组织和利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”共同宣判，其中，其被重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，并处罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日；其余<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人亦被分别枉法判处<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月—<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月不等刑期。目前疑似在四川省成都龙泉驿监狱服刑<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/12/5.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/12/5.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">23/</span></b></span></span><a name="_Hlk175715609"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">田奇庄</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">1953</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日出生，河北省保定市人，中共党员，前《峰峰矿工报》和《中国煤炭报》记者，河北省作家协会和杂文协会会员，知名网络专栏作家，独立中文笔会会员，前北京非政治组织机构“公盟”理事（之一）及行政主管，邯郸市区人大代表参选人，实名举报人，民主宪政追求者和宪政之路践行者，中国在押政治犯。早期曾为下乡知青，返城后曾当过矿工等基础工人；<span lang="EN-US">1984</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-1993</span>年，曾先后在邯郸市《峰峰矿工报》和《中国煤炭报》当记者；从业期间，因工作敬业，成绩斐然，而曾多次获得企业、矿务局、邯郸市、河北省新闻协会和中国煤炭报先进个人称号；<span lang="EN-US">1993</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-2007</span>年，曾先后任邯郸市赵都商场办公室主任、乐颐房地产公司办公室主任及锦江房地产公司副总经理等职；<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-2004</span>年，曾被邯郸市政府聘为行风监督员，多次向政府部门提出有关参政议政意见和建议，并开始积极参选区人大代表选举；自<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年起，在办理提前退休手续后，曾在北京非政治组织机构“公盟”担任理事（之一），并做法律研究者及行政主管；退休后，因在《中国选举与治理网》、《博客中国》、《凯迪网络》、《中国改革网》等多家网站当专栏作家，并在报社和网络上发表近千篇文章，观念影响甚广，故而备受专家学者赞赏，且被网友誉为“网络大侠”、“启蒙先锋”；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，曾因向中纪委实名举报，广西自治区党委在书记刘宁主持下搞个人崇拜，而遭河北省邯郸市警方搜查抄家；同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，又因与另两位老党员董洪义、马贵全联合在中共“二十大”前夕发公开信，呼吁“修改党章、党政分离、防杜个人崇拜”，遂被邯郸市警方悉数传唤带走，几天之后，其与董洪义被以涉嫌“勾结外国势力”罪由正式刑拘，马贵全因身体出现眩晕而被取保候审后遣回北京原籍；后其与董洪义<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人被邯郸市检察院以同罪由正式批捕；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日获悉，其<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人案已被邯郸市检察院移交到邯郸市法院，并应于本月庭审；据悉，其辩护律师为法院指派，并或因“新帐”、“旧账”一起算而被重判；其本人已被单位停发工资，其姊受牵连而被当地政府以“手续不合法”为由从自家购买的农家院驱逐。目前被羁押于河北邯郸磁县看守所（河北省邯郸市磁县磁州镇西湖街，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">056500</span>）。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月获悉，田奇庄先生获刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月。田奇庄及董洪义均关押在河北省邯郸监狱。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/blog-post_10.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/blog-post_10.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/01/2.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">男，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">51</span>岁，昆明市官渡区双桥村人。曾因修炼法轮功被劳教两年，<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半，还遭关洗脑班<span lang="EN-US">1</span>次。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日下午，法轮功学员张晓华到官渡区子君路星云园小区朋友家串门，被警方抓捕，随后张晓华家被搜查。同时被抓捕的还有田云波、李萍等人。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日张晓华、李萍、田云波被五华区法院视频庭审，后被判刑：张晓华<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，李萍<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月，田云波<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。田云波刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span><a _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吴国芹</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">北京怀柔区法轮功学员，</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">2022</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，北京怀柔区出动大批警察大面积抓捕法轮功学员，早上<span lang="EN-US">7</span>点多钟，统一开始了抓捕抄家。大约有吴国芹等二十多人。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月得知法轮功学员吴国芹被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，目前已被关押到大兴女子监狱。<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/6/18/462097.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日分别被佳木斯市向阳区法院视频远程庭审，于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月中旬下达判决书，判刘广有<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年有期徒刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p lang="EN-US">7</span>年，张桂英被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。张桂英刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">32/</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">张建华：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黑龙江加格达奇法轮功学员，女。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被加格达奇曙光派出所抓捕。知情人说，因为张建华给人讲真相，被跟踪，被警察抄家并抓捕。警察从她家里抢走法轮功相关书籍等私人财产。因警察抢劫现金，张建华的儿子制止。几天后，她儿子竟被以“袭警”为名抓捕。家人费尽周折，儿子才被放回。张建华一直被羁押在加格达奇看守所，后被加格达奇区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日早被送往黑龙江省女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/4/445762.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/4/445762.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">33/</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><b 0pt;">赵树霞：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">天津市滨海新区大港法轮功学，女，<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年生。自<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共迫害法轮功以来，赵树霞因为坚持修炼法轮功，曾被多次迫害，先后两次被劳教、<span lang="EN-US">1</span>次判刑，累计遭冤狱迫害<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年多。第<span lang="EN-US">2</span>次被劳教时她绝食抗议<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多，身体极度虚弱，期间被强行灌食，冬天包夹犯人把窗户打开折磨她。最后她被迫害致生命垂危，最后警察无奈放人回家。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，赵树霞去天津市区办事，被天津市南开区国保抓捕、关押，然后警察又到大港赵树霞的母亲家抄家。有知情人透露，抓捕构陷她的原因只是因为她给警察写了一封劝善信。后两次被开庭，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月中旬获悉她已被劫持到天津女子监狱。据家人说她被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/7/445902.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/7/445902.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><b 0pt;">周秀丽</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：山西省忻州市代县法轮功女学员，<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日出生。周秀丽在去内蒙古探望失去生活自理能力的老母亲期间，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日在包头市城区发放法轮功资料时被包头市达茂联合旗公安局国保大队抓捕。同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日被代县公安局执行逮捕并关押在忻州市看守所遭受迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日被判刑期<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">6</span>千元，给家庭造成很大的压力和伤害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">长春市法轮功学员，女。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被二道区分局国保大队警察抓捕。现获知，杨金凤被判刑<span
