New Roman&quot;;">13/</span></b></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">徐琳：</span></b></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">广州民主人士、词曲作家、人权捍卫者<a name="_Hlk175814045">徐琳</a>先生的关押地广州市南沙区看守所已于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日搬迁新址<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，本网获悉：广州民主人士、词曲作家、人权捍卫者徐琳先生的关押地广州市南沙区看守所已于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日搬迁新址，新址地址：广州市南沙区榄核镇启安街<span lang="EN-US">1</span>号，看守所会见服务电话<span lang="EN-US">020-34876544</span>，<span lang="EN-US">17728081668</span>。人权捍卫者徐琳先生是于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日遭广州市公安局南沙区分局以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪刑事拘留的，一个月后其已经被正式批捕。一直羁押在广州市南沙看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">徐琳简介：</span></b></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1964</span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年出生，湖南省株洲市人，诗人，哲学研究者，广东网络作家，独立中文笔会成员，民主异议人士，中国良心犯。自<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年代末即开始撰写时政文章，诗歌及创作歌曲，至<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年始又在广州，深圳等地积极开展街头举牌，演讲，组织公民集会等活动<span lang="EN-US">;</span>近年来，因与维权公民刘四仿合作，创作并出品了多个以自由，人权，法治为内容的歌曲，颇受自由民主爱好者喜爱与欢迎，遂引起广东当局强烈不满，并成为维稳严控的对象，曾遭多次非法拘禁和秘密关押<span lang="EN-US">;2012</span>年，曾因将浙江异见人士朱虞夫所作诗歌“是时候了”改编谱曲为“就是现在”，引起网友广泛关注和转载而被广州警方于同年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪“刑拘，羁押于广州市番禹看守所，指控其罪行比广州上街举牌还要严重，具有明显煽动群众上街意向，情节十分严重<span lang="EN-US">;</span>后于<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日又被广东省当局改为秘密监视居住它处，期间其家属多次要求当局出示书面通知及关押地点，竟都遭拒<span lang="EN-US">;</span>同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，曾参与民主人士王登朝发起的<span lang="EN-US">'</span>莲花山公园千人公民集会<span lang="EN-US">'</span>，计划于活动现场发表政治演讲，不料事前却遭当局绑架，后被秘密关押<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月<span lang="EN-US">;2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，曾因发布“<span lang="EN-US">709</span>”大抓捕事件而创作的歌曲“正义律师之歌”触怒当局，其任职公司因受当局施压而遭失业，并被绑架至广州软禁<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，中共<span lang="EN-US">19</span>大召开前夕，其在湖南老家照顾患病父亲时突然被广州市南沙区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘，其广州住所被查抄，搜走计算机，手机，书籍，笔记本等个人物品；次日，与其一起创作歌曲的搭档刘四方也被江西省宜春市警方以同理由抓走；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，被广州市南沙区检察院以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”正式批捕，关押在广州市南沙区看守所；据悉，被押期间遭酷刑，从<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日—<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日每天都被警方三班倒提讯；一直零口供；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，被广州市南沙区法院以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。此前其在东省佛山市高明监狱服刑。徐琳先生又于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日遭广州市公安局南沙区分局以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日获悉，其已经被正式批捕。一直羁押在广州市南沙看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/08/2024731.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/08/2024731.html</span></b></span></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">14/</span></b></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">季孝龙：</span></b></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">获刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月的著名人权捍卫者季孝龙已于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日转监到上海市提篮桥监狱<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，本网获悉：获刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月的著名人权捍卫者季孝龙已于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日转监到上海市提篮桥监狱（青浦区西庆路<span lang="EN-US">709</span>号）服刑，监狱邮编<span lang="EN-US">20082</span>，总机<span lang="EN-US">55589900</span>，<span lang="EN-US">39207780</span>。此前，季孝龙先被转至判刑人员“集训”地——上海市新收犯监狱进行所谓“集训”。在上海市新收犯监狱期间，季孝龙一直未能获得家人会见。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">季孝龙简介：</span></b></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1976</span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日出生，江苏省张家港市人，张家港市杨舍镇名都花苑居民，基督徒，维权公民，民主人士，人权捍卫者，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，曾因宣传民主理念而被上海市浦东新区警方以“寻衅滋事”罪由传唤，并被处以行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，曾因在网上发文，呼吁民主人士响应“厕所革命”，并在医院、大学等公共场所的厕所门上，用马克笔写宣传语“大病治不起，习胖狂撒币，修宪妄称帝、苦难何时毕！打倒共产党。还政于民，结束民众苦难。推翻习核心，拒走文革路”等字句，短时间内响应者众多，随于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日再次被浦东新区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留；同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，又被送到指定居所监视居住；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，被以同罪由转正式逮捕，关押在上海市浦东新区看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，其案被上海市浦东新区检察院起诉至上海市浦东新区法院；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，其最终被该法院以“寻衅滋事罪”一审判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，后送上海市白茅岭监狱七监区服刑；据悉，羁押期间，警方曾多次以让其“死亡”和用寒冷气温逼迫其认罪，致其身体健康虚弱且生病吐血；其家属曾送羽绒服和《圣经》书籍亦遭拒收；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日刑满获释；同年上海封城，其为上海市民持续发声。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，再次被上海市梅园新村派出所警察从家中带走，后被上海市浦东新区警方以“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，又被浦东新检察院以同罪名正式批捕，后季孝龙于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被起诉。后已经开庭，未宣判。最终于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，被一些寻衅滋事罪判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，此前被羁押于浦东新区看守所，后转监至上海市新收犯监狱，最后，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日转监到上海市提篮桥监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"></span></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/08/462024722.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/08/462024722.html</span></b></span></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">15/</span></b></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">朱玉芳：</span></b></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">获刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年的江西维权人士朱玉芳狱中遭殴打后留下严重后遗症，病痛缠身，得不到有效治疗，狱中申诉遭到扣压延宕<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，本网近日获悉：被以“寻衅滋事”罪名判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年的江西维权人士朱玉芳，自今年在其服刑的江西省女子监狱遭到同监舍犯人殴打后，留下严重后遗症，头部被击打后至今仍然时常头痛、失眠，胸部疼痛憋闷，手部关节僵硬疼痛。朱玉芳病痛缠身，在狱中没有有效治疗，又得不到保外就医。狱方将其作为重点犯人，严加看管，朱玉芳在狱中提交申诉，被要求限期补充证据材料，但补充证据的通知，不知被何人何故长时间扣压延宕，当朱玉芳收到通知时早已经过了补充材料的期限，致使申诉无效。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">朱玉芳简介：</span></b></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">朱玉芳是江西萍乡的强拆维权者。曾是经营<span lang="EN-US">4</span>家店面的私营业主，<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年拆迁中，萍乡市政府主要领导亲属开办的房地产公司拒不兑现拆迁协议，朱玉芳被迫走上维权之路。在维权过程中，她不仅自己维权，也积极帮助他人维权，呼吁社会公正，遂被地方政府视为重点维稳控制和打击对象，被多次截访绑架、关黑监狱、遭受酷刑。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年，朱玉芳因在北京身穿“没有腐败就没有访民”的文化衫维权，被北京警方抓走，转交给江西萍乡安源区警方以“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘，后被萍乡市安源区法院以“寻衅滋事”罪名判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年出狱后，朱玉芳一直为被枉法冤判而申诉；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，她到江西省高级法院申诉，遭拒，遂在法院门外举牌呼吁；一周后的<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日（世界人权日），朱玉芳就被萍乡市警方抓捕，随即被以“寻衅滋事”罪名刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，朱玉芳第二次被萍乡市安源区法院以“寻衅滋事”罪名判刑，这次刑期比上次更长——<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。上诉后，萍乡市中级法院二审裁决维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。朱玉芳因为被枉法判刑而申诉喊冤，结果却遭到更大打击，被加重判刑。中共当局的司法由此可见一斑。朱玉芳在江西省女子监狱的通讯地址：江西省南昌市新建县<span lang="EN-US">916</span>信箱<span lang="EN-US">4</span>分箱（江西省女子监狱四监区）朱玉芳，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">330100</span>，电话：<span lang="EN-US">0791-83718743</span>。江西省女子监狱地址：江西省南昌市新建县长堎镇长征路<span lang="EN-US">630</span>号江西省女子监狱。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"></span></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/08/4_7.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/08/4_7.html</span></b></span></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">16/</span></b></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><b><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈剑雄：</span></b></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">获刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年的湖北省赤壁市民主人士陈剑雄转监至湖北省咸宁监狱服刑<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，本网获悉：获刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年的湖北省赤壁市民主人士陈剑雄（本名陈进新）与<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被转监至湖北省咸宁监狱服刑，地址：湖北省咸宁市桂乡大道特<span lang="EN-US">6</span>号，邮编：<span lang="EN-US">437100</span>。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈剑雄（本名陈进新）简介：</span></b></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1974</span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年出生，湖北省赤壁市人，网名陈剑雄，“赤壁五君子”之一，南方街头运动践行者，民主维权公民，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170539327;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk173203427;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">自<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年以来，曾多次参与国内的围观声援活动，勇于多次举牌、拉横幅表达对民主宪政的政治要求，是南方街头运动杰出代表之一，亦因此曾多次遭到中共警方的拘留、刑拘、酷刑和强行驱赶等；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，曾因与袁小华、袁奉初、黄文勋等民主维权者在湖北省赤壁市宣传民主政治，而被当地警方以“煽动颠覆国家政权”为由刑拘，<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日被取保获释；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，曾与民主维权者谢文飞在广东省佛山市街头举横幅，要求“废除一党专制，建立民主中国”，而被佛山警方再次以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”刑拘，并关押在天河区看守所，备受酷刑折磨，<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被取保获释；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月，曾因参加山东曲阜薛福顺非正常死亡事件观察团奔赴曲阜追查真相，多次在曲阜遭警方殴打和驱赶；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，曾因到黑龙江省声援“建三江律师被拘事件”，而被当警方行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，曾因到武汉市与多名友人会见佛教法师徐志强，被武汉警方抓走，又被以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”刑拘，<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被取保候审；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，因再次前往河南郑州参与公民声援“郑州十君子事件”，并到河南焦作市声援“张小玉夫妇杀警事件”，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被警方在郑州第三看守所附近抓走，且被湖北省赤壁市警方直接报检察院以涉嫌“扰乱社会公共秩序罪”执行逮捕，羁押于赤壁市看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，被湖北省咸宁市赤壁市法院以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，刑满释放；出狱后，其追求民主意志弥坚；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，因与维权友人袁兵、梁一鸣去赤壁市公安局国保大队投诉出狱后遭长期监控、骚扰等事宜，终因双方理念不同、争论激烈而不欢而散；<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，再次被赤壁市警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”抓捕刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，被赤壁市检察院正式批捕，并被羁押于赤壁看守所：<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，终被湖北省赤壁市法院一审以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；其不服上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，经咸宁市中级法院二审裁决，依然维持原判；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，刑满释放。此前在湖北省咸宁监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日陈剑雄又被当地警方刑事拘留，后被批捕<span lang="EN-US">,</span>罪名是寻衅滋事。后遭起诉，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日开庭审理，未宣判。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日宣判，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。此前被羁押在湖北赤壁市看守所，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被转监到湖北省咸宁监狱服刑（地址：湖北省咸宁市桂乡大道特<span lang="EN-US">6</span>号，邮编：<span lang="EN-US">437100</span>）。<b>信息来源： <span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、方艺融：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US">30</span>日</a>，湖南娄底青年方艺融效法四通桥勇士彭立发在湖南娄底新化县天桥悬挂四通桥标语：不要特权要平等，不要封控要自由，不要谎言要尊严，不要文革要改革……用扩音器播放：要自由，要民主，要选票；罢工，罢课，罢免独裁国贼习近平！据目前已被中共湖南当局抓捕。<a name="_Hlk175817942"><b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></a></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175817942;"></span></span><a lang="EN-US">(</span>曾用网名春天）因第一个从境外网站转发勇士方艺融拉横幅视频到其所在微信群”卵谈群“而被刑事拘留，“卵谈群”群友随后差不多都被问话。此拉横幅事件令中共当局极为恐慌，据称公安部已派员进驻湖南办案，各地加大维稳力度，防止类似事件在其他地区再现。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">王伟明、</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1/</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">部金香：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">内蒙古赤峰市人，女，法轮功学员，租住在北京大兴区。部金香因用手机发法轮功内容微信，于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被大兴公安局抓捕，关押在大兴区看守所构陷，后被刑事拘留、批捕、起诉，最终被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年。判刑后部金香被转监北京女子监狱。部金香在北京女子监狱三监区期间，遭肉体与精神折磨及药物迫害，被折磨至精神失常、目光呆滞、臃肿、衰老不堪，完全换了一个人。有消息说，目前她精神正常，但仍被狱方逼吃治疗精神类药物，每天三顿饭后睁不开眼，需要靠墙闭眼睡一会。即使这样，她每天仍被迫干奴工活。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，齐志银在北京的女儿家中被警察抓捕，又被关押到天津武清区看守所。当地公、检、法人员对齐志银合伙构陷，历经刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月获悉，齐志银已于<span &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">：山东省烟台市莱阳市法轮功学员，女，家住莱阳市山前店镇宋家庄村。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年五十多岁。因修炼法轮功其多次遭中共人员骚扰、抓捕和迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，山前店镇派出所警察闯到孙成荣家对其抄家抓捕，并将孙成荣关押到烟台市福山看守所。随即遭刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月底，孙成荣被转监到位于济南市的山东省女子监狱迫害。据宋家庄村干部称，孙成荣被法院判了七年重刑。刑期至<span 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">山东省莱西市姜山镇法轮功学员，女，蒙古族人，一九八四年二月十日出生，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">40</span>岁。吴佳健及家人原居住于辽宁省阜新市，她的父母于一九九六年开始修炼法轮功。一九九九年七月中共迫害法轮功后，吴佳健一家因坚持修炼法轮功，经常遭到中共人员的骚扰。<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年底，她的父母被当地警察抓捕、拘留、勒索。后来一家人只得被迫背井离乡，流离失所，几经磨难、周折，最后居移到山东青岛莱西市姜山镇。河南省洛阳市警察从<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月期间，跨省绑架了二十多位法轮功学员，以在网上传播法轮功为由，对这些法轮功学员判以重刑。吴佳健就是其中一人。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日晚十八时，吴佳健被以查身份证名义闯入家中的七个警察抓捕。随即吴佳健被河南洛阳国保拉走，带到河南，关押在洛阳市看守所，后遭批捕、并以吴佳健通过微信转发法轮功视频起诉至洛阳市涧西区法院。此后，吴佳健便信息全无。直到<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年，她的家人才得知，吴佳健被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">5/</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">龚瑞平：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">北京法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1965</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日生，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年五十九岁，原北京市平谷区大华山小学教师，家住北京市平谷区刘家店镇刘家店村。龚瑞平一九九六年五月份开始修炼法轮功。一九九九年七月中共发动了疯狂迫害法轮功的政治运动。龚瑞平女士因坚持法轮功信仰，遭到中共残酷迫害，被开除教师工作，被强制离婚，多次被绑架，三次被关洗脑班，两次被劳教，两次被判刑，在共计<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月监禁中她饱受酷刑折磨。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，龚瑞平因宣讲法轮功遭人举报，在租住地被警察抓捕，被关押在顺义看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，龚瑞平被平谷区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚款一万一千元。龚瑞平已经被转监到北京女子监狱。据知情人士透露，龚瑞平被迫害不让睡觉休息。监狱为了迫害法轮功学员，每个去厕所的人都会叫法轮功学员陪同，用这种方式不让睡觉，每夜被“无数次”的叫醒，根本无法休息。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月获悉，龚瑞平因坚持不“转化”，被狱方迫害致半身麻木，被送到监狱医院继续迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">山东省临沂市沂南县法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1967</span>年生，原沂南县化肥厂职工，<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年王洪梅开始修炼法轮功。王洪梅因坚持修炼，曾在拘留所、洗脑班、劳教所遭受迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年王洪梅被劳教三年，在山东省第一女子劳教所遭残酷迫害——遭狱警的电击、熬鹰等多种酷刑摧残。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，王洪梅当地警方抓捕、抄家，随后王洪梅被劫持到沂南县拘留所行政拘留十五天。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，王洪梅被行政拘留关押到期，又被转为刑事拘留。随后被批捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日前后，王红梅在沂南县法院被庭审。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月初获悉：王洪梅被沂南县法院判刑五年后，随后被转监济南女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">：云南省昆明市的法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1957</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">67</span>岁。昆明市土产公司退休职工，暂住在昆明市西山区海口镇山冲石城北村。早年修炼法轮功，在中共迫害法轮功的二十五年中，郭伶多次遭到警察绑架、抄家，曾被枉判十一年，两次在云南省第二女子监狱遭受迫害，她被关禁闭，长时间罚坐小凳等，被迫害致股骨头坏死，出狱时，她不能行走。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">郭伶<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日遭西山公安分局、海口派出所人员抓捕、关押，半年后被“取保候审”。此后一年中，她频繁遭国保、派出所警察、检察院人员跟踪、骚扰、罗织构陷材料。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，郭伶遭昆明市西山区法院非法判刑四年。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，其被强制身体检查，法院决定对其收监关进监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/08/4_28.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/08/4_28.html</span></b></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><a name="_Hlk175814232"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">8/</span></b></a></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175814232;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘玉琴</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175814232;"></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">：甘肃庆阳市法轮功学员，女，原是庆城县陇东中学一级教师，<span lang="EN-US">1961</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">61</span>岁。刘玉琴一九九八年四月开始修炼法轮功。因为其坚持修炼法轮功，在中共江泽民一伙发动的对法轮功的迫害中，她于<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年被判刑三年，<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年被学校开除。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年至<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年，刘玉琴被关押在甘肃省女子监狱，身心遭受了极度摧残，身体骨瘦如柴，一度随时有生命危险。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，刘玉琴在高楼乡发法轮功资料时被人举报，遭警方抓捕并抄家，后刘玉琴被关押进宁县看守所。随即遭刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日遭镇原县法院开庭，律师为她做无罪辩护。刘玉琴也当庭表示自己无罪。近悉，刘玉琴被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/08/4_10.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/08/4_10.html</span></b></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">9/</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">杨兴理：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">吉林省舒兰市法轮功学员，男，吉林市下辖舒兰市吉舒镇人。杨兴理因坚持修炼法轮功，多次被中共绑架、关押、劳教、被关精神病院，遭上电刷子酷刑折磨，为生存不得不搬到长春市榆树地区居住多年。杨兴理被开除公职后，生活拮据，精神受到严重创伤一度出现精神失常。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，在吉林市政府门前，杨兴理又被吉林市站前派出所警察抓捕，后被关押在吉林看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月中旬获悉：杨兴理被当地法院秘密判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"></span><a lang="EN-US">1953</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">71</span>岁。家住潍坊市坊子区九龙街办菜园村。中共一九九九年七月开始疯狂迫害法轮功学员，朱天富一家人也多次遭迫害，朱天富曾被判刑五年，妻子张希美在王村劳教所被迫害致精神失常。朱天富<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被当地警察抓捕到洗脑班关押，<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被潍坊市坊子区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，当时由于疫情的缘故他被放回了家。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，潍坊市坊子分局警察将朱天富抓捕收监到潍坊看守所。这是朱天富第二次被中共法院判刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US">10</span>月因遭人举报被南定派出所警察抓捕了李景花，警察因当时的疫情对她实施取保候审一年。期间当地国保大队对老人进行司法构陷，于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月将李景花老人抓捕到淄博市看守所。随即张店法院对李景花老人判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元。目前李景花老人已经被转监到济南女子监狱迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：<span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">福建省厦门市集美区法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1973</span>年生。福建省武平县人，后居住厦门市集美区，她曾是一位中学教师。<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，中共江泽民流氓集团开始迫害法轮功与修炼者，王菊香<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年底背着三个月大的孩子上京为法轮功说句公道话，回来后警方将她交给学校监管。<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，王菊香在武平县城书写“法轮功好”、“真善忍”等真相标语，向学生讲天安门自焚骗局，被迫害关押，因不放弃信仰，最后被判刑三年。王菊香<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被国保警察入室抓捕，第二天傍晚她被释放回家，她被监视居住。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，王菊香被刑事拘留关押到看守所，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月并处罚金，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，她被转监关押至福建省女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，刘桂兰被正阳派出所警察抓捕，警察称她在禄人小区发放法轮功资料被监控录像拍到。随即刘桂兰被关押到拘留所。刘桂兰<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月被德惠市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，已被转监到吉林省女子监狱迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b lang="EN-US">5</span>日，刘淑花因拒绝所谓“转化”又被转移到潍坊看守所继续关押。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月末获悉：刘淑花被诸城市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/08/blog-post_41.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">21/</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李俊：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">四川成都市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日成都公安局温江区分局抓捕了成都市法轮功学员段琼英、李涛、于川程、徐月琴、李俊、罗义等多人，他们先被秘密拘禁于新津洗脑班。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，这六位法轮功学员被逮捕，并被转入成都郫县看守所及温江看守所，涉嫌罪名也从“煽动颠覆国家政权”被改为“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日遭温江区法院开庭宣判：其中段琼英<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；李涛<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；于川程<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年；徐月琴<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月；罗义<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月；李俊<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月；并处罚金。这些法轮功学员都提出上诉。李俊刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/08/blog-post_41.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">22/</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">赵建华：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">河北平泉维权人士，赵春红的兄长，男，<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日出生，汉族，初中文化，住址：河北省平泉市南五十家子镇五十家子村。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年初，赵建华开始到南五十家子镇政府反映失地保险问题，但问题始终未得到解决。其无奈之下只好前往北京信访，被平泉警方多次拦截带回后拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，赵建华被平泉市公安局口头告知，其被以扰乱公共秩序处于行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。其妹赵春红为投资矿产被大股东侵吞股权事于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日到国家信访局上访。到<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，赵春红的家人收到了河北省平泉市公安局以“涉嫌寻衅滋事罪”对她刑事拘留通知，并告知已将赵春红在承德看守所关押。后其兄长赵建华也因为失地维权，被当地警方以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪刑事拘留。赵春红被控寻衅滋事案于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日在隆化县法院第一法庭开庭，未判。赵春红的哥哥赵建华因为失地维权被控寻衅滋事罪，于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日在平泉市法院开庭审理，一审获刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。其不服上诉，二审维持原判，平泉法院判处赵建华退还此前政府向其支付的养老保险金。赵建华目前关押在平泉市看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">郭美学</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">:</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">山东省烟台市龙口市法轮功学员<span lang="EN-US">,</span>男。郭美学因坚持法轮信仰，曾被中共关押到山东省第二劳教所劳教两年，期间遭到关禁闭室、被电击、吊铐、饿饭等残酷折磨。郭美学因宣讲法轮功遭人举报，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被龙口市公安局国保警察抓捕，关押在看守所。之后，在龙口市政法委、“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”的操控下，龙口市法院于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日对郭美学进行庭审，之后对他判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。目前郭美学仍被关押在龙口市张家沟看守所，被狱警铐着手铐、脚镣。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"></span><a &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">陕西西安市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1958</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年六十六岁。家住陕西省西安市雁塔区，她近年到重庆帮女儿带孩子。赵力女士于一九九七年开始修炼法轮功。中共一九九九年七月开始迫害法轮功，赵力也遭到中共的绑架、关押，曾于<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年被劳动教养<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半、<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年半。赵力女士因邮寄一封宣传法轮功的信，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日在重庆被警察抓捕、抄家，对其刑事拘留，但当晚让她以“取保候审”回家。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，赵力被重庆市江北区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月，随即遭收监被关押在重庆市渝北区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年初，赵力被转监到重庆市女子监狱，至今已八个月，狱方一直不让家属接见，也不让给生活费。家人不知赵力近况，非常担忧。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘玉玲：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">山东德州市法轮功学员，女。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日早晨，德州市德城区国保大队和新河东路派出所、湖滨北路派出所等几个派出所统一行动，抓捕了德州当地法轮功学员刘玉玲、赵玉才、路秀铭等十几人，并抄了他们的家，所有被绑架的法轮功学员均被关押到德州看守所。这是山东省德州市当局对法轮功学员的一次大规模的迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月获悉，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，德州市德城区法院判刘玉玲<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，赵玉才<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，路秀铭<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月，并罚金不等。刘玉玲刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/08/19.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><a name="_Hlk175812386"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：</span></b></span><span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日早晨，德州市德城区国保大队和新河东路派出所、湖滨北路派出所等几个派出所统一行动，抓捕了德州当地法轮功学员刘玉玲、赵玉才、路秀铭等十几人，并抄了他们的家，所有被绑架的法轮功学员均被关押到德州看守所。这是山东省德州市当局对法轮功学员的一次大规模的迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月获悉，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，德州市德城区法院判刘玉玲<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，赵玉才<span &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/08/16_18.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">27/</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">胡艳：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">山东省淄博市张店区南定镇法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1969</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">55</span>岁。因修炼法轮功，她被迫害过三次，身陷囹圄近六年，被罚金一万元。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日上午，胡艳被五名国保警察突然闯进家中抄家、抓捕，警察抄走了整套法轮功书籍，还有电脑、打印机等私人财物。胡艳第二天被取保候审回家，被要求每月定时到国保大队去汇报。胡艳<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月在某小区发真相资料，被人举报。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，她被派出所抓捕并抄家，后取保获释；<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，她再次被抓捕，随即被关押。后遭批捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月获悉，胡艳女士已经被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，已被转监到济南女子监狱迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/08/16.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/08/16.html</span></b></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">山东德州市法轮功学员，女。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日早晨，德州市德城区国保大队和新河东路派出所、湖滨北路派出所等几个派出所统一行动，抓捕了德州当地法轮功学员刘玉玲、赵玉才、路秀铭、张文艳等十几人，并抄了他们的家，所有被绑架的法轮功学员均被关押到德州看守所。这是山东省德州市当局对法轮功学员的一次大规模的迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月获悉，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，德州市德城区法院判刘玉玲<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，赵玉才<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，路秀铭<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月，并罚金不等。路秀铭刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"></span><a 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">王伟明：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">北京市房山区法轮功学员，男，家住北京市房山区石楼镇夏村。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，王伟明在北京市房山区石楼镇二站村发放法轮功资料，被北京市公安局房山分局石楼派出所警车行车记录仪拍到，石楼派出所警察将他抓捕，并抄家。当天，王伟明被劫往燕山“预审中心”。第二天，<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，警察欲将王伟明关押到房山看守所，因他身体检查不合格，被看守所拒收，后被警方以所谓“取保候审”放回家。后当地公检法相互勾结、构陷，王伟明被北京市房山区法院判刑一年，于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日晚被北京市房山区法院警察抓捕收监。现王伟明被关押在位于房山区长阳那边的新看守所服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: lang="EN-US">A</span>、<span lang="EN-US">B</span>、<span lang="EN-US">C</span>、<span lang="EN-US">D</span>、<span lang="EN-US">E</span>、<span lang="EN-US">F.....X</span>、<span lang="EN-US">Y</span>、<span lang="EN-US">Z</span>）。查询者可依据姓名的第一个拼音字母，即可查询到相关人员姓名，而其简介均可在报告中查找到。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span
